We will showcase how to deal with this with both </span><span data-offset-key="aada12da81384564b4f955bad3297019:1">`os.path.join`</span><span data-offset-key="aada12da81384564b4f955bad3297019:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="aada12da81384564b4f955bad3297019:3">`pathlib.Path.joinpath`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4b035f766fa14bc7b67f5170d7011b57"><span data-offset-key="4b035f766fa14bc7b67f5170d7011b57:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="4b035f766fa14bc7b67f5170d7011b57:1">`os.path.join`</span><span data-offset-key="4b035f766fa14bc7b67f5170d7011b57:2"> on Windows:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os​>>> os.path.join('usr', 'bin', 'spam')'usr\\bin\\spam'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6f77e77318044e9aaac2619e8aca9fc8"><span data-offset-key="6f77e77318044e9aaac2619e8aca9fc8:0">And using </span><span data-offset-key="6f77e77318044e9aaac2619e8aca9fc8:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="6f77e77318044e9aaac2619e8aca9fc8:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path​>>> print(Path('usr').joinpath('bin').joinpath('spam'))usr/bin/spam

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="527b677a0b7a42e3a4c4dc858b17367e"><span data-offset-key="527b677a0b7a42e3a4c4dc858b17367e:0">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="527b677a0b7a42e3a4c4dc858b17367e:1"> also provides a shortcut to joinpath using the </span><span data-offset-key="527b677a0b7a42e3a4c4dc858b17367e:2">`/`</span><span data-offset-key="527b677a0b7a42e3a4c4dc858b17367e:3"> operator:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path​>>> print(Path('usr') / 'bin' / 'spam')usr/bin/spam

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="32efa1cbf2d54dcc8bb4d518ee41aa7c"><span data-offset-key="32efa1cbf2d54dcc8bb4d518ee41aa7c:0">Notice the path separator is different between Windows and Unix based operating system, that's why you want to use one of the above methods instead of adding strings together to join paths together.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5a84ce36870b491891fcbd5da3b34894"><span data-offset-key="5a84ce36870b491891fcbd5da3b34894:0">Joining paths is helpful if you need to create different file paths under the same directory.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="69748adf506c4b21b632d30461c74ab9"><span data-offset-key="69748adf506c4b21b632d30461c74ab9:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="69748adf506c4b21b632d30461c74ab9:1">`os.path.join`</span><span data-offset-key="69748adf506c4b21b632d30461c74ab9:2"> on Windows:</span></span></span>

    >>> my_files = ['accounts.txt', 'details.csv', 'invite.docx']​>>> for filename in my_files:>>>     print(os.path.join('C:\\Users\\asweigart', filename))C:\Users\asweigart\accounts.txtC:\Users\asweigart\details.csvC:\Users\asweigart\invite.docx

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3ce31c8be4fe4567b2f5eb6e5cf0234a"><span data-offset-key="3ce31c8be4fe4567b2f5eb6e5cf0234a:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="3ce31c8be4fe4567b2f5eb6e5cf0234a:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="3ce31c8be4fe4567b2f5eb6e5cf0234a:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> my_files = ['accounts.txt', 'details.csv', 'invite.docx']>>> home = Path.home()>>> for filename in my_files:>>>     print(home / filename)/home/asweigart/accounts.txt/home/asweigart/details.csv/home/asweigart/invite.docx

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a9829e5cc5cc434ea9025a6969547531"><span data-offset-key="a9829e5cc5cc434ea9025a6969547531:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="28163fafd3154d429f8d568e5c0a9ab6"><span data-offset-key="28163fafd3154d429f8d568e5c0a9ab6:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="4857f1a4f15048e8937f817327dcef25"><span data-offset-key="4857f1a4f15048e8937f817327dcef25:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8dac1949815a45f5a8ff9bf47cceb266"><span data-offset-key="8dac1949815a45f5a8ff9bf47cceb266:0">The Current Working Directory</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ae033b7b97664e31a0129bc960c71c1f"><span data-offset-key="ae033b7b97664e31a0129bc960c71c1f:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="ae033b7b97664e31a0129bc960c71c1f:1">`os`</span><span data-offset-key="ae033b7b97664e31a0129bc960c71c1f:2"> on Windows:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os​>>> os.getcwd()'C:\\Python34'>>> os.chdir('C:\\Windows\\System32')​>>> os.getcwd()'C:\\Windows\\System32'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4478cdb14cba4c5992ec80e6719e2e28"><span data-offset-key="4478cdb14cba4c5992ec80e6719e2e28:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="4478cdb14cba4c5992ec80e6719e2e28:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="4478cdb14cba4c5992ec80e6719e2e28:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> from os import chdir​>>> print(Path.cwd())/home/asweigart​>>> chdir('/usr/lib/python3.6')>>> print(Path.cwd())/usr/lib/python3.6

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7698ccac4b23452499c26d130eeed2b0"><span data-offset-key="7698ccac4b23452499c26d130eeed2b0:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3549060f806f4d9bbc4cd62f7d8d8874"><span data-offset-key="3549060f806f4d9bbc4cd62f7d8d8874:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="83f3c3afec454a438f6be73de8fb93b0"><span data-offset-key="83f3c3afec454a438f6be73de8fb93b0:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="80bd9842201341dd9cd9a06ec736b0d8"><span data-offset-key="80bd9842201341dd9cd9a06ec736b0d8:0">Creating New Folders</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="08bc39fb1e614c9391ad4462c0a97830"><span data-offset-key="08bc39fb1e614c9391ad4462c0a97830:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="08bc39fb1e614c9391ad4462c0a97830:1">`os`</span><span data-offset-key="08bc39fb1e614c9391ad4462c0a97830:2"> on Windows:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> os.makedirs('C:\\delicious\\walnut\\waffles')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2d3e4842cc2f463f8a807e156824024d"><span data-offset-key="2d3e4842cc2f463f8a807e156824024d:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="2d3e4842cc2f463f8a807e156824024d:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="2d3e4842cc2f463f8a807e156824024d:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> cwd = Path.cwd()>>> (cwd / 'delicious' / 'walnut' / 'waffles').mkdir()Traceback (most recent call last):  File "<stdin>", line 1, in <module>  File "/usr/lib/python3.6/pathlib.py", line 1226, in mkdir    self._accessor.mkdir(self, mode)  File "/usr/lib/python3.6/pathlib.py", line 387, in wrapped    return strfunc(str(pathobj), *args)FileNotFoundError: [Errno 2] No such file or directory: '/home/asweigart/delicious/walnut/waffles'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a7d35eb8d1334e8b84610aef377bba89"><span data-offset-key="a7d35eb8d1334e8b84610aef377bba89:0">Oh no, we got a nasty error! The reason is that the 'delicious' directory does not exist, so we cannot make the 'walnut' and the 'waffles' directories under it. To fix this, do:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> cwd = Path.cwd()>>> (cwd / 'delicious' / 'walnut' / 'waffles').mkdir(parents=True)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="661d8788543e4e2fba4f03f4267a567b"><span data-offset-key="661d8788543e4e2fba4f03f4267a567b:0">And all is good :)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5506db83cb2b41efab37129085247717"><span data-offset-key="5506db83cb2b41efab37129085247717:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ee06b335c3b84ac4a79bb8ee12e991fa"><span data-offset-key="ee06b335c3b84ac4a79bb8ee12e991fa:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="adddbbf5d62b4b0b91a188330ea4c054"><span data-offset-key="adddbbf5d62b4b0b91a188330ea4c054:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f49e47b47218424dbe1c6d345c31739e"><span data-offset-key="f49e47b47218424dbe1c6d345c31739e:0">Absolute vs. Relative Paths</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9accc9245c62459f83fb560a83002589"><span data-offset-key="9accc9245c62459f83fb560a83002589:0">There are two ways to specify a file path.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a86e7267a8fd40598ad75f233eac95c9"><span data-offset-key="a86e7267a8fd40598ad75f233eac95c9:0">An absolute path, which always begins with the root folder</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="71efb53462bc4c1b8d0c5fe1700eff14"><span data-offset-key="71efb53462bc4c1b8d0c5fe1700eff14:0">A relative path, which is relative to the program’s current working directory</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="78cbe5ade2014e4a939163a87d88f9d5"><span data-offset-key="78cbe5ade2014e4a939163a87d88f9d5:0">There are also the dot (.) and dot-dot (..) folders. These are not real folders but special names that can be used in a path. A single period (“dot”) for a folder name is shorthand for “this directory.” Two periods (“dot-dot”) means “the parent folder.”</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="422089a92bb1464b869dfcfa8b7823ca"><span data-offset-key="422089a92bb1464b869dfcfa8b7823ca:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5b2790351598458085cb7fe34977202e"><span data-offset-key="5b2790351598458085cb7fe34977202e:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="646152c2dd004130839f743fbc0ecb10"><span data-offset-key="646152c2dd004130839f743fbc0ecb10:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="54b786bb76ee471da35874dff7e04761"><span data-offset-key="54b786bb76ee471da35874dff7e04761:0">Handling Absolute and Relative Paths</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d8826f8754fb4afb992d116dbd5badbe"><span data-offset-key="d8826f8754fb4afb992d116dbd5badbe:0">To see if a path is an absolute path:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1d6a34bacdb64f2498bc5bc363c487c0"><span data-offset-key="1d6a34bacdb64f2498bc5bc363c487c0:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="1d6a34bacdb64f2498bc5bc363c487c0:1">`os.path`</span><span data-offset-key="1d6a34bacdb64f2498bc5bc363c487c0:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> os.path.isabs('/')True>>> os.path.isabs('..')False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1a2eab5af3314693b8161e25177a18ee"><span data-offset-key="1a2eab5af3314693b8161e25177a18ee:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="1a2eab5af3314693b8161e25177a18ee:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="1a2eab5af3314693b8161e25177a18ee:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> Path('/').is_absolute()True>>> Path('..').is_absolute()False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b481e7d874ab4f8890289f938ebda93c"><span data-offset-key="b481e7d874ab4f8890289f938ebda93c:0">You can extract an absolute path with both </span><span data-offset-key="b481e7d874ab4f8890289f938ebda93c:1">`os.path`</span><span data-offset-key="b481e7d874ab4f8890289f938ebda93c:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="b481e7d874ab4f8890289f938ebda93c:3">`pathlib`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe8cd9e7cd2c457c893b839b4ebcc78d"><span data-offset-key="fe8cd9e7cd2c457c893b839b4ebcc78d:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="fe8cd9e7cd2c457c893b839b4ebcc78d:1">`os.path`</span><span data-offset-key="fe8cd9e7cd2c457c893b839b4ebcc78d:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> os.getcwd()'/home/asweigart'>>> os.path.abspath('..')'/home'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a16a88bcc6a44892b9edcb5e3c8fecec"><span data-offset-key="a16a88bcc6a44892b9edcb5e3c8fecec:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="a16a88bcc6a44892b9edcb5e3c8fecec:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="a16a88bcc6a44892b9edcb5e3c8fecec:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    from pathlib import Pathprint(Path.cwd())/home/asweigartprint(Path('..').resolve())/home

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a714ccca27a547f09acb1baf8a7d7d86"><span data-offset-key="a714ccca27a547f09acb1baf8a7d7d86:0">You can get a relative path from a starting path to another path.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="24a008dbf5e64f049b7999b730f1b205"><span data-offset-key="24a008dbf5e64f049b7999b730f1b205:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="24a008dbf5e64f049b7999b730f1b205:1">`os.path`</span><span data-offset-key="24a008dbf5e64f049b7999b730f1b205:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> os.path.relpath('/etc/passwd', '/')'etc/passwd'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ad91aa7e7c5e4e4c97d59092d4b17166"><span data-offset-key="ad91aa7e7c5e4e4c97d59092d4b17166:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="ad91aa7e7c5e4e4c97d59092d4b17166:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="ad91aa7e7c5e4e4c97d59092d4b17166:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> print(Path('/etc/passwd').relative_to('/'))etc/passwd

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="51cf631e054d417bab6ce1db54f1b55c"><span data-offset-key="51cf631e054d417bab6ce1db54f1b55c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a00eeb683eea41b986d1876c2384b995"><span data-offset-key="a00eeb683eea41b986d1876c2384b995:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="5316a7f695344aed96bfee78f2e360a3"><span data-offset-key="5316a7f695344aed96bfee78f2e360a3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d226ad0991584052affaa528d205aced"><span data-offset-key="d226ad0991584052affaa528d205aced:0">Checking Path Validity</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="875f6ae695ef494b8fb02f3fe6d20092"><span data-offset-key="875f6ae695ef494b8fb02f3fe6d20092:0">Checking if a file/directory exists:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b1d31f9201994d358f19e46a21250c44"><span data-offset-key="b1d31f9201994d358f19e46a21250c44:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="b1d31f9201994d358f19e46a21250c44:1">`os.path`</span><span data-offset-key="b1d31f9201994d358f19e46a21250c44:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    import os>>> os.path.exists('.')True>>> os.path.exists('setup.py')True>>> os.path.exists('/etc')True>>> os.path.exists('nonexistentfile')False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f3ebd116d18f44c78ddf84958ba63672"><span data-offset-key="f3ebd116d18f44c78ddf84958ba63672:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="f3ebd116d18f44c78ddf84958ba63672:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="f3ebd116d18f44c78ddf84958ba63672:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    from pathlib import Path>>> Path('.').exists()True>>> Path('setup.py').exists()True>>> Path('/etc').exists()True>>> Path('nonexistentfile').exists()False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="779e14e2415241e29e1d5c1953e0c2d1"><span data-offset-key="779e14e2415241e29e1d5c1953e0c2d1:0">Checking if a path is a file:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6366c4c3724543e5903b580a2d56867e"><span data-offset-key="6366c4c3724543e5903b580a2d56867e:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="6366c4c3724543e5903b580a2d56867e:1">`os.path`</span><span data-offset-key="6366c4c3724543e5903b580a2d56867e:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> os.path.isfile('setup.py')True>>> os.path.isfile('/home')False>>> os.path.isfile('nonexistentfile')False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5ebd77365e47456dbe973bf7f560212a"><span data-offset-key="5ebd77365e47456dbe973bf7f560212a:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="5ebd77365e47456dbe973bf7f560212a:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="5ebd77365e47456dbe973bf7f560212a:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> Path('setup.py').is_file()True>>> Path('/home').is_file()False>>> Path('nonexistentfile').is_file()False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e2cad39fc9f9464f962ac72cf4f7ba68"><span data-offset-key="e2cad39fc9f9464f962ac72cf4f7ba68:0">Checking if a path is a directory:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7613bc951c514f49baf307f3085a2063"><span data-offset-key="7613bc951c514f49baf307f3085a2063:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="7613bc951c514f49baf307f3085a2063:1">`os.path`</span><span data-offset-key="7613bc951c514f49baf307f3085a2063:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> os.path.isdir('/')True>>> os.path.isdir('setup.py')False>>> os.path.isdir('/spam')False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="666d15ec74ac447b9b2e71fe8c520b82"><span data-offset-key="666d15ec74ac447b9b2e71fe8c520b82:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="666d15ec74ac447b9b2e71fe8c520b82:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="666d15ec74ac447b9b2e71fe8c520b82:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> Path('/').is_dir()True>>> Path('setup.py').is_dir()False>>> Path('/spam').is_dir()False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="23f00aa37f4a47a482de89c4881cff6f"><span data-offset-key="23f00aa37f4a47a482de89c4881cff6f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7ba832145b40448480e9df971d576ee3"><span data-offset-key="7ba832145b40448480e9df971d576ee3:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="9609e080bc284baeadb7f6de5db0a8c7"><span data-offset-key="9609e080bc284baeadb7f6de5db0a8c7:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="545ed6bfc69e4d8383eefde37c17234a"><span data-offset-key="545ed6bfc69e4d8383eefde37c17234a:0">Finding File Sizes and Folder Contents</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f69d1d3a701e4bc5b3b9d38658abb00f"><span data-offset-key="f69d1d3a701e4bc5b3b9d38658abb00f:0">Getting a file's size in bytes:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0fb648491ba14e73b5bf75ab30895d2a"><span data-offset-key="0fb648491ba14e73b5bf75ab30895d2a:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="0fb648491ba14e73b5bf75ab30895d2a:1">`os.path`</span><span data-offset-key="0fb648491ba14e73b5bf75ab30895d2a:2"> on Windows:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> os.path.getsize('C:\\Windows\\System32\\calc.exe')776192

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a17a6d74f17143409d6a43eb68f4d3fd"><span data-offset-key="a17a6d74f17143409d6a43eb68f4d3fd:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="a17a6d74f17143409d6a43eb68f4d3fd:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="a17a6d74f17143409d6a43eb68f4d3fd:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> stat = Path('/bin/python3.6').stat()>>> print(stat) # stat contains some other information about the file as wellos.stat_result(st_mode=33261, st_ino=141087, st_dev=2051, st_nlink=2, st_uid=0,--snip--st_gid=0, st_size=10024, st_atime=1517725562, st_mtime=1515119809, st_ctime=1517261276)>>> print(stat.st_size) # size in bytes10024

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5ead5f7788b04a1696970d05e2ae7b41"><span data-offset-key="5ead5f7788b04a1696970d05e2ae7b41:0">Listing directory contents using </span><span data-offset-key="5ead5f7788b04a1696970d05e2ae7b41:1">`os.listdir`</span><span data-offset-key="5ead5f7788b04a1696970d05e2ae7b41:2"> on Windows:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> os.listdir('C:\\Windows\\System32')['0409', '12520437.cpx', '12520850.cpx', '5U877.ax', 'aaclient.dll',--snip--'xwtpdui.dll', 'xwtpw32.dll', 'zh-CN', 'zh-HK', 'zh-TW', 'zipfldr.dll']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="44895c3a8e0f4323b6d220d6b7babceb"><span data-offset-key="44895c3a8e0f4323b6d220d6b7babceb:0">Listing directory contents using </span><span data-offset-key="44895c3a8e0f4323b6d220d6b7babceb:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="44895c3a8e0f4323b6d220d6b7babceb:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> for f in Path('/usr/bin').iterdir():>>>     print(f).../usr/bin/tiff2rgba/usr/bin/iconv/usr/bin/ldd/usr/bin/cache_restore/usr/bin/udiskie/usr/bin/unix2dos/usr/bin/t1reencode/usr/bin/epstopdf/usr/bin/idle3...

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f40c8b1807d74c4585cf5a7c04830c72"><span data-offset-key="f40c8b1807d74c4585cf5a7c04830c72:0">To find the total size of all the files in this directory:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ac0d5a5053245769413e23218eee784"><span data-offset-key="2ac0d5a5053245769413e23218eee784:0">**WARNING**</span><span data-offset-key="2ac0d5a5053245769413e23218eee784:1">: Directories themselves also have a size! So you might want to check for whether a path is a file or directory using the methods in the methods discussed in the above section!</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ee6d5643c5b94203bf49b04153de40fb"><span data-offset-key="ee6d5643c5b94203bf49b04153de40fb:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="ee6d5643c5b94203bf49b04153de40fb:1">`os.path.getsize()`</span><span data-offset-key="ee6d5643c5b94203bf49b04153de40fb:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="ee6d5643c5b94203bf49b04153de40fb:3">`os.listdir()`</span><span data-offset-key="ee6d5643c5b94203bf49b04153de40fb:4"> together on Windows:</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> total_size = 0​>>> for filename in os.listdir('C:\\Windows\\System32'):      total_size = total_size + os.path.getsize(os.path.join('C:\\Windows\\System32', filename))​>>> print(total_size)1117846456

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5c5dcf1d4df440a1872c4902bd41aeaf"><span data-offset-key="5c5dcf1d4df440a1872c4902bd41aeaf:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="5c5dcf1d4df440a1872c4902bd41aeaf:1">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="5c5dcf1d4df440a1872c4902bd41aeaf:2"> on \*nix:</span></span></span>

    >>> from pathlib import Path>>> total_size = 0​>>> for sub_path in Path('/usr/bin').iterdir():...     total_size += sub_path.stat().st_size>>>>>> print(total_size)1903178911

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eaf1f02b3ca84efaa903b2aa2e6df454"><span data-offset-key="eaf1f02b3ca84efaa903b2aa2e6df454:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b3347267c0634b9abaf3aa18655724a8"><span data-offset-key="b3347267c0634b9abaf3aa18655724a8:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="2bcc07dcd6da4217b541918973ef81c6"><span data-offset-key="2bcc07dcd6da4217b541918973ef81c6:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="20123f8fb47d4f7996ed471888a50e85"><span data-offset-key="20123f8fb47d4f7996ed471888a50e85:0">Copying Files and Folders</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d7188c97f6ac4c8b8dffd42657793a8c"><span data-offset-key="d7188c97f6ac4c8b8dffd42657793a8c:0">The shutil module provides functions for copying files, as well as entire folders.</span></span></span>

    >>> import shutil, os​>>> os.chdir('C:\\')​>>> shutil.copy('C:\\spam.txt', 'C:\\delicious')   'C:\\delicious\\spam.txt'​>>> shutil.copy('eggs.txt', 'C:\\delicious\\eggs2.txt')   'C:\\delicious\\eggs2.txt'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="78ed7c9f776f4776837240c967b894ad"><span data-offset-key="78ed7c9f776f4776837240c967b894ad:0">While shutil.copy() will copy a single file, shutil.copytree() will copy an entire folder and every folder and file contained in it:</span></span></span>

    >>> import shutil, os​>>> os.chdir('C:\\')​>>> shutil.copytree('C:\\bacon', 'C:\\bacon_backup')'C:\\bacon_backup'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e8152fae47334f17a6364dc3220a833e"><span data-offset-key="e8152fae47334f17a6364dc3220a833e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fcfa3bae6f8f45bda1d3f28a5bd117af"><span data-offset-key="fcfa3bae6f8f45bda1d3f28a5bd117af:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="b53ef628de3b4553a48ad599dbc353d3"><span data-offset-key="b53ef628de3b4553a48ad599dbc353d3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="db2518701e1a44d7bca5a0747c37cbfe"><span data-offset-key="db2518701e1a44d7bca5a0747c37cbfe:0">Moving and Renaming Files and Folders</span></span></span>

    >>> import shutil>>> shutil.move('C:\\bacon.txt', 'C:\\eggs')'C:\\eggs\\bacon.txt'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="345a355c334f4974b0574f5ad22d6649"><span data-offset-key="345a355c334f4974b0574f5ad22d6649:0">The destination path can also specify a filename. In the following example, the source file is moved and renamed:</span></span></span>

    >>> shutil.move('C:\\bacon.txt', 'C:\\eggs\\new_bacon.txt')'C:\\eggs\\new_bacon.txt'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1fb40ca0a57f4e409b00d9c775ccd18f"><span data-offset-key="1fb40ca0a57f4e409b00d9c775ccd18f:0">If there is no eggs folder, then move() will rename bacon.txt to a file named eggs.</span></span></span>

    >>> shutil.move('C:\\bacon.txt', 'C:\\eggs')'C:\\eggs'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bd2d309c617e41f78b4dd677fc48d58b"><span data-offset-key="bd2d309c617e41f78b4dd677fc48d58b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="29b26ecc40a64708982026db47580426"><span data-offset-key="29b26ecc40a64708982026db47580426:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="d73d6ba0767e43c5997b0b6a62d7fec9"><span data-offset-key="d73d6ba0767e43c5997b0b6a62d7fec9:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b1dc87cb46e4e2abb3e04fd4d584659"><span data-offset-key="9b1dc87cb46e4e2abb3e04fd4d584659:0">Permanently Deleting Files and Folders</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="237137a6cd5b4713acd8a9e8d1a27528"><span data-offset-key="237137a6cd5b4713acd8a9e8d1a27528:0">Calling os.unlink(path) or Path.unlink() will delete the file at path.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0d18b132d88d438aa9480c7599337c92"><span data-offset-key="0d18b132d88d438aa9480c7599337c92:0">Calling os.rmdir(path) or Path.rmdir() will delete the folder at path. This folder must be empty of any files or folders.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c1a400eb90074cf48048b92187f2ad96"><span data-offset-key="c1a400eb90074cf48048b92187f2ad96:0">Calling shutil.rmtree(path) will remove the folder at path, and all files and folders it contains will also be deleted.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e766eb26294346bba94a8b29cfb49b8e"><span data-offset-key="e766eb26294346bba94a8b29cfb49b8e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="19c2dccff2134598a39ca5f05f84a36e"><span data-offset-key="19c2dccff2134598a39ca5f05f84a36e:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="642f9de4a0ef4f1584dae1c31ef96405"><span data-offset-key="642f9de4a0ef4f1584dae1c31ef96405:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e5e4acb69bd248c8b83c93647a5e8198"><span data-offset-key="e5e4acb69bd248c8b83c93647a5e8198:0">Safe Deletes with the send2trash Module</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3d99e3ad7bda48dc9fb2688c92fabacf"><span data-offset-key="3d99e3ad7bda48dc9fb2688c92fabacf:0">You can install this module by running pip install send2trash from a Terminal window.</span></span></span>

    >>> import send2trash​>>> with open('bacon.txt', 'a') as bacon_file: # creates the file...     bacon_file.write('Bacon is not a vegetable.')25​>>> send2trash.send2trash('bacon.txt')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4d9c8a0084aa437b86fb8d1953605e21"><span data-offset-key="4d9c8a0084aa437b86fb8d1953605e21:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="848cab562c264765827bf561250254ec"><span data-offset-key="848cab562c264765827bf561250254ec:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="2cea52e319f34b2e8049229f760fe19b"><span data-offset-key="2cea52e319f34b2e8049229f760fe19b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7179ec900fd740a88a06917e7e9a65e1"><span data-offset-key="7179ec900fd740a88a06917e7e9a65e1:0">Walking a Directory Tree</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>>>>> for folder_name, subfolders, filenames in os.walk('C:\\delicious'):>>>     print('The current folder is {}'.format(folder_name))>>>>>>     for subfolder in subfolders:>>>         print('SUBFOLDER OF {}: {}'.format(folder_name, subfolder))>>>     for filename in filenames:>>>         print('FILE INSIDE {}: {}'.format(folder_name, filename))>>>>>>     print('')The current folder is C:\deliciousSUBFOLDER OF C:\delicious: catsSUBFOLDER OF C:\delicious: walnutFILE INSIDE C:\delicious: spam.txt​The current folder is C:\delicious\catsFILE INSIDE C:\delicious\cats: catnames.txtFILE INSIDE C:\delicious\cats: zophie.jpg​The current folder is C:\delicious\walnutSUBFOLDER OF C:\delicious\walnut: waffles​The current folder is C:\delicious\walnut\wafflesFILE INSIDE C:\delicious\walnut\waffles: butter.txt

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="97b94ed7364a426abaa2ad1e87e0dae4"><span data-offset-key="97b94ed7364a426abaa2ad1e87e0dae4:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6d1c75f116054618a366f23d5914d723"><span data-offset-key="6d1c75f116054618a366f23d5914d723:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="2cf5d9039d55449e900b44f0a18a1805"><span data-offset-key="2cf5d9039d55449e900b44f0a18a1805:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9188a566007a445ebee34818d1ccb878"><span data-offset-key="9188a566007a445ebee34818d1ccb878:0">`pathlib`</span><span data-offset-key="9188a566007a445ebee34818d1ccb878:1"> provides a lot more functionality than the ones listed above, like getting file name, getting file extension, reading/writing a file without manually opening it, etc. Check out the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/pathlib.html" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5a043ec8e04a4f8e9a81df43f51988ec"><span data-offset-key="5a043ec8e04a4f8e9a81df43f51988ec:0">official documentation</span></span></a><span data-key="f43b02273a8040ae8b4794b1b02ffcc6"><span data-offset-key="f43b02273a8040ae8b4794b1b02ffcc6:0"> if you want to know more!</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bef75f691e134a098f237d7a79c4a936"><span data-offset-key="bef75f691e134a098f237d7a79c4a936:0">Reading and Writing Files</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ed0cbfe7c3624a4e81a1a119ff261160"><span data-offset-key="ed0cbfe7c3624a4e81a1a119ff261160:0">The File Reading/Writing Process</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5613cfb5f93c42a4a646f4702562db76"><span data-offset-key="5613cfb5f93c42a4a646f4702562db76:0">To read/write to a file in Python, you will want to use the </span><span data-offset-key="5613cfb5f93c42a4a646f4702562db76:1">`with`</span><span data-offset-key="5613cfb5f93c42a4a646f4702562db76:2"> statement, which will close the file for you after you are done.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0544b6c7ebf14d2389fed583aab3115c"><span data-offset-key="0544b6c7ebf14d2389fed583aab3115c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="12fe90aa79b349a785faf60ca2d5e798"><span data-offset-key="12fe90aa79b349a785faf60ca2d5e798:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="d1f0df06f93f40358ba98680ab29d30e"><span data-offset-key="d1f0df06f93f40358ba98680ab29d30e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="40404e20ba12484db3fdee6e7782b1b4"><span data-offset-key="40404e20ba12484db3fdee6e7782b1b4:0">Opening and reading files with the open() function</span></span></span>

    >>> with open('C:\\Users\\your_home_folder\\hello.txt') as hello_file:...     hello_content = hello_file.read()>>> hello_content'Hello World!'​>>> # Alternatively, you can use the *readlines()* method to get a list of string values from the file, one string for each line of text:​>>> with open('sonnet29.txt') as sonnet_file:...     sonnet_file.readlines()[When, in disgrace with fortune and men's eyes,\n', ' I all alone beweep myoutcast state,\n', And trouble deaf heaven with my bootless cries,\n', Andlook upon myself and curse my fate,']​>>> # You can also iterate through the file line by line:>>> with open('sonnet29.txt') as sonnet_file:...     for line in sonnet_file: # note the new line character will be included in the line...         print(line, end='')​When, in disgrace with fortune and men's eyes,I all alone beweep my outcast state,And trouble deaf heaven with my bootless cries,And look upon myself and curse my fate,

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8e5e3f8a167a43058f1379cfbaf57614"><span data-offset-key="8e5e3f8a167a43058f1379cfbaf57614:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e2201ab0f19c407a99cb8fd7f29aca5c"><span data-offset-key="e2201ab0f19c407a99cb8fd7f29aca5c:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="85cc55b6843a4bf884134c9c3c6a169b"><span data-offset-key="85cc55b6843a4bf884134c9c3c6a169b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="16928625ff394e3980182b388fb20119"><span data-offset-key="16928625ff394e3980182b388fb20119:0">Writing to Files</span></span></span>

    >>> with open('bacon.txt', 'w') as bacon_file:...     bacon_file.write('Hello world!\n')13​>>> with open('bacon.txt', 'a') as bacon_file:...     bacon_file.write('Bacon is not a vegetable.')25​>>> with open('bacon.txt') as bacon_file:...     content = bacon_file.read()​>>> print(content)Hello world!Bacon is not a vegetable.

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eb5448b0c80c4d409049a24b06c90dcb"><span data-offset-key="eb5448b0c80c4d409049a24b06c90dcb:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="54573c0fc70246cc8f6cf18c2a778372"><span data-offset-key="54573c0fc70246cc8f6cf18c2a778372:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="dcb6515140b6400d9f11378e48f03089"><span data-offset-key="dcb6515140b6400d9f11378e48f03089:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="48f84b4c13c14f30aa33091a4f8be8c3"><span data-offset-key="48f84b4c13c14f30aa33091a4f8be8c3:0">Saving Variables with the shelve Module</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="05853930ffa74a7b8673d14924cadd38"><span data-offset-key="05853930ffa74a7b8673d14924cadd38:0">To save variables:</span></span></span>

    >>> import shelve​>>> cats = ['Zophie', 'Pooka', 'Simon']>>> with shelve.open('mydata') as shelf_file:...     shelf_file['cats'] = cats

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e6d280e50cdf4119ae1a287b2dfdf27e"><span data-offset-key="e6d280e50cdf4119ae1a287b2dfdf27e:0">To open and read variables:</span></span></span>

    >>> with shelve.open('mydata') as shelf_file:...     print(type(shelf_file))...     print(shelf_file['cats'])<class 'shelve.DbfilenameShelf'>['Zophie', 'Pooka', 'Simon']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="35db7ba9e2d84d44acbd7f7a73f30781"><span data-offset-key="35db7ba9e2d84d44acbd7f7a73f30781:0">Just like dictionaries, shelf values have keys() and values() methods that will return list-like values of the keys and values in the shelf. Since these methods return list-like values instead of true lists, you should pass them to the list() function to get them in list form.</span></span></span>

    >>> with shelve.open('mydata') as shelf_file:...     print(list(shelf_file.keys()))...     print(list(shelf_file.values()))['cats'][['Zophie', 'Pooka', 'Simon']]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d3b18cdf39d84266ad1c67ca4fb2fb7e"><span data-offset-key="d3b18cdf39d84266ad1c67ca4fb2fb7e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b789ee7055cf41b58cc364150e418408"><span data-offset-key="b789ee7055cf41b58cc364150e418408:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="03f1b3d1194647ff81847b9a5c6ef032"><span data-offset-key="03f1b3d1194647ff81847b9a5c6ef032:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8f5fee455c504b99b2ac74dff0168905"><span data-offset-key="8f5fee455c504b99b2ac74dff0168905:0">Saving Variables with the pprint.pformat() Function</span></span></span>

    >>> import pprint​>>> cats = [{'name': 'Zophie', 'desc': 'chubby'}, {'name': 'Pooka', 'desc': 'fluffy'}]​>>> pprint.pformat(cats)"[{'desc': 'chubby', 'name': 'Zophie'}, {'desc': 'fluffy', 'name': 'Pooka'}]"​>>> with open('myCats.py', 'w') as file_obj:...     file_obj.write('cats = {}\n'.format(pprint.pformat(cats)))83

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7c5d2efe22274d0590cb92dff2c51499"><span data-offset-key="7c5d2efe22274d0590cb92dff2c51499:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f344d96c7abc43a0b74115af34f26c26"><span data-offset-key="f344d96c7abc43a0b74115af34f26c26:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="cb26275878644fb99867dfc91629467e"><span data-offset-key="cb26275878644fb99867dfc91629467e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4a790ed4c7ed491da4c93d9fd1059567"><span data-offset-key="4a790ed4c7ed491da4c93d9fd1059567:0">Reading ZIP Files</span></span></span>

    >>> import zipfile, os​>>> os.chdir('C:\\')    # move to the folder with example.zip>>> with zipfile.ZipFile('example.zip') as example_zip:...     print(example_zip.namelist())...     spam_info = example_zip.getinfo('spam.txt')...     print(spam_info.file_size)...     print(spam_info.compress_size)...     print('Compressed file is %sx smaller!' % (round(spam_info.file_size / spam_info.compress_size, 2)))​['spam.txt', 'cats/', 'cats/catnames.txt', 'cats/zophie.jpg']139083828'Compressed file is 3.63x smaller!'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a65bfd0209a34018bbf04da6545eec8d"><span data-offset-key="a65bfd0209a34018bbf04da6545eec8d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0db4a37cceed4a449412b2e8f01c6339"><span data-offset-key="0db4a37cceed4a449412b2e8f01c6339:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="bafd845e22524eb88c08f2f4490d6f90"><span data-offset-key="bafd845e22524eb88c08f2f4490d6f90:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="82900e3569514ac4879b40132fed7652"><span data-offset-key="82900e3569514ac4879b40132fed7652:0">Extracting from ZIP Files</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c5f139b456924d268c88499a9ea97c5b"><span data-offset-key="c5f139b456924d268c88499a9ea97c5b:0">The extractall() method for ZipFile objects extracts all the files and folders from a ZIP file into the current working directory.</span></span></span>

    >>> import zipfile, os​>>> os.chdir('C:\\')    # move to the folder with example.zip​>>> with zipfile.ZipFile('example.zip') as example_zip:...     example_zip.extractall()

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="891d92ed942642cc871a74760765a038"><span data-offset-key="891d92ed942642cc871a74760765a038:0">The extract() method for ZipFile objects will extract a single file from the ZIP file. Continue the interactive shell example:</span></span></span>

    >>> with zipfile.ZipFile('example.zip') as example_zip:...     print(example_zip.extract('spam.txt'))...     print(example_zip.extract('spam.txt', 'C:\\some\\new\\folders'))'C:\\spam.txt''C:\\some\\new\\folders\\spam.txt'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="07a75fa407104dcbbf31f0c112c5d6e8"><span data-offset-key="07a75fa407104dcbbf31f0c112c5d6e8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f8746409306b443193e58338ceabf54b"><span data-offset-key="f8746409306b443193e58338ceabf54b:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="bf5d84f4fef1436181c280168e46a81f"><span data-offset-key="bf5d84f4fef1436181c280168e46a81f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="47cff1177e7c403b80481145c5164084"><span data-offset-key="47cff1177e7c403b80481145c5164084:0">Creating and Adding to ZIP Files</span></span></span>

    >>> import zipfile​>>> with zipfile.ZipFile('new.zip', 'w') as new_zip:...     new_zip.write('spam.txt', compress_type=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2cd6559ddbde4a43825de74c408499c9"><span data-offset-key="2cd6559ddbde4a43825de74c408499c9:0">This code will create a new ZIP file named new.zip that has the compressed contents of spam.txt.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="687915097d2448dca284647086bb8109"><span data-offset-key="687915097d2448dca284647086bb8109:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="accab5379832438494a58aef1bf104ca"><span data-offset-key="accab5379832438494a58aef1bf104ca:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="48044c8f49bd4204b484dc8ef2c7067a"><span data-offset-key="48044c8f49bd4204b484dc8ef2c7067a:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="62b6aec123e84efc83169d4a557ada42"><span data-offset-key="62b6aec123e84efc83169d4a557ada42:0">JSON, YAML and configuration files</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b4c2dcd94ef24547b0cde51c036fbbba"><span data-offset-key="b4c2dcd94ef24547b0cde51c036fbbba:0">JSON</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7918665d4f884feba36748614c939c25"><span data-offset-key="7918665d4f884feba36748614c939c25:0">Open a JSON file with:</span></span></span>

    import jsonwith open("filename.json", "r") as f:    content = json.loads(f.read())

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="39488c57f44c4b0e9627ddc1b2d3d491"><span data-offset-key="39488c57f44c4b0e9627ddc1b2d3d491:0">Write a JSON file with:</span></span></span>

    import json​content = {"name": "Joe", "age": 20}with open("filename.json", "w") as f:    f.write(json.dumps(content, indent=2))

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6b92d645d3634853aa575cc52b844112"><span data-offset-key="6b92d645d3634853aa575cc52b844112:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0eb6545e495d421fbb91340fc6512984"><span data-offset-key="0eb6545e495d421fbb91340fc6512984:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="6276b56c6e9e4f98ba152597e14b85b9"><span data-offset-key="6276b56c6e9e4f98ba152597e14b85b9:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="67ea4f98a315413f86d5f4dce6155663"><span data-offset-key="67ea4f98a315413f86d5f4dce6155663:0">YAML</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="14246f1c435d40be86edd35d330ba5a0"><span data-offset-key="14246f1c435d40be86edd35d330ba5a0:0">Compared to JSON, YAML allows for much better human maintainability and gives you the option to add comments. It is a convenient choice for configuration files where humans will have to edit it.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b33b4aa959194acc9e55c78e53048258"><span data-offset-key="b33b4aa959194acc9e55c78e53048258:0">There are two main libraries allowing to access to YAML files:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="919648f92def48a2bdb2dc6d02ba0121"><span data-offset-key="919648f92def48a2bdb2dc6d02ba0121:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pypi.python.org/pypi/PyYAML" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="59613c086e8947bcbc717e6dc0d0f69c"><span data-offset-key="59613c086e8947bcbc717e6dc0d0f69c:0">PyYaml</span></span></a><span data-key="569b9e6e379f47a0bb0e4ea3a7dc4814"><span data-offset-key="569b9e6e379f47a0bb0e4ea3a7dc4814:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="082e52bb733e4050bfba8496ecac4821"><span data-offset-key="082e52bb733e4050bfba8496ecac4821:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pypi.python.org/pypi/ruamel.yaml" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b64ad275df2e48bfa1513fa71d9e4eba"><span data-offset-key="b64ad275df2e48bfa1513fa71d9e4eba:0">Ruamel.yaml</span></span></a><span data-key="aa94142e0b4d4600adceff3934759e2b"><span data-offset-key="aa94142e0b4d4600adceff3934759e2b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4ff3fca84dcb474fb68bb81490afbffb"><span data-offset-key="4ff3fca84dcb474fb68bb81490afbffb:0">Install them using </span><span data-offset-key="4ff3fca84dcb474fb68bb81490afbffb:1">`pip install`</span><span data-offset-key="4ff3fca84dcb474fb68bb81490afbffb:2"> in your virtual environment.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5058b020b3d44e8c8288840784c4bd87"><span data-offset-key="5058b020b3d44e8c8288840784c4bd87:0">The first one it easier to use but the second one, Ruamel, implements much better the YAML specification, and allow for example to modify a YAML content without altering comments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3bc5f5acfe5d480799b76b52bc03c54f"><span data-offset-key="3bc5f5acfe5d480799b76b52bc03c54f:0">Open a YAML file with:</span></span></span>

    from ruamel.yaml import YAML​with open("filename.yaml") as f:    yaml=YAML()    yaml.load(f)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fba85cf3ceab4a6db4c5cdd43dc775c9"><span data-offset-key="fba85cf3ceab4a6db4c5cdd43dc775c9:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="78e3668485e34de5bfd686839e127dd5"><span data-offset-key="78e3668485e34de5bfd686839e127dd5:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="69a85f83c41e4501a49f5d9e367551ad"><span data-offset-key="69a85f83c41e4501a49f5d9e367551ad:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="38ba393cb1124a26a6dd806d4a5c7894"><span data-offset-key="38ba393cb1124a26a6dd806d4a5c7894:0">Anyconfig</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7df6fd3d85e34c8da02c4705fd5023ed"><span data-offset-key="7df6fd3d85e34c8da02c4705fd5023ed:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pypi.python.org/pypi/anyconfig" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a9d9132772a84fe7a28819f07b926b5b"><span data-offset-key="a9d9132772a84fe7a28819f07b926b5b:0">Anyconfig</span></span></a><span data-key="dd07f003d0dc40f3adf4c1b1d2c87f2f"><span data-offset-key="dd07f003d0dc40f3adf4c1b1d2c87f2f:0"> is a very handy package allowing to abstract completely the underlying configuration file format. It allows to load a Python dictionary from JSON, YAML, TOML, and so on.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dffa3f8540fe43baa0116fd905dfc9fc"><span data-offset-key="dffa3f8540fe43baa0116fd905dfc9fc:0">Install it with:</span></span></span>

    pip install anyconfig

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c308276184954e8a8cd84e4db3f5fb7d"><span data-offset-key="c308276184954e8a8cd84e4db3f5fb7d:0">Usage:</span></span></span>

    import anyconfig​conf1 = anyconfig.load("/path/to/foo/conf.d/a.yml")

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b4dcc5dd33a74615aa74c65ebefc3009"><span data-offset-key="b4dcc5dd33a74615aa74c65ebefc3009:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3cb9a617f17c47b5a973d242be7c5623"><span data-offset-key="3cb9a617f17c47b5a973d242be7c5623:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="b9f17921947342d083b91b44d67cdc80"><span data-offset-key="b9f17921947342d083b91b44d67cdc80:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fddb14f7b2ec4f77b0d1a5f248c81d96"><span data-offset-key="fddb14f7b2ec4f77b0d1a5f248c81d96:0">Debugging</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8d0291fb739c4624b10afebfe9cf8475"><span data-offset-key="8d0291fb739c4624b10afebfe9cf8475:0">Raising Exceptions</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="aa64671a64de49e49de544cf71fe9253"><span data-offset-key="aa64671a64de49e49de544cf71fe9253:0">Exceptions are raised with a raise statement. In code, a raise statement consists of the following:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a421fe0bbd1b4a0cb61dbf457d07944e"><span data-offset-key="a421fe0bbd1b4a0cb61dbf457d07944e:0">The raise keyword</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="570561dad2f3434d981019c2769b5501"><span data-offset-key="570561dad2f3434d981019c2769b5501:0">A call to the Exception() function</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="39261e59aade45cd9dc41b1a0d5b582f"><span data-offset-key="39261e59aade45cd9dc41b1a0d5b582f:0">A string with a helpful error message passed to the Exception() function</span></span></span>

    >>> raise Exception('This is the error message.')Traceback (most recent call last):  File "<pyshell#191>", line 1, in <module>    raise Exception('This is the error message.')Exception: This is the error message.

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1bb61c15ca194c3ca1646261a9a2de9b"><span data-offset-key="1bb61c15ca194c3ca1646261a9a2de9b:0">Often it’s the code that calls the function, not the function itself, that knows how to handle an exception. So you will commonly see a raise statement inside a function and the try and except statements in the code calling the function.</span></span></span>

    def box_print(symbol, width, height):    if len(symbol) != 1:      raise Exception('Symbol must be a single character string.')    if width <= 2:      raise Exception('Width must be greater than 2.')    if height <= 2:      raise Exception('Height must be greater than 2.')    print(symbol * width)    for i in range(height - 2):        print(symbol + (' ' * (width - 2)) + symbol)    print(symbol * width)for sym, w, h in (('*', 4, 4), ('O', 20, 5), ('x', 1, 3), ('ZZ', 3, 3)):    try:        box_print(sym, w, h)    except Exception as err:        print('An exception happened: ' + str(err))

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d780691c5e084c2daf3e08011e7058af"><span data-offset-key="d780691c5e084c2daf3e08011e7058af:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="53d87a5648704af4bd0dae373fea5bbd"><span data-offset-key="53d87a5648704af4bd0dae373fea5bbd:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="3ef2553758da440299b27d9be8d47b57"><span data-offset-key="3ef2553758da440299b27d9be8d47b57:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9e1ee15c4dbc4455a35a34daf860575b"><span data-offset-key="9e1ee15c4dbc4455a35a34daf860575b:0">Getting the Traceback as a String</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0dd4d9048bb54afbb71045f2747a9b43"><span data-offset-key="0dd4d9048bb54afbb71045f2747a9b43:0">The traceback is displayed by Python whenever a raised exception goes unhandled. But can also obtain it as a string by calling traceback.format\_exc(). This function is useful if you want the information from an exception’s traceback but also want an except statement to gracefully handle the exception. You will need to import Python’s traceback module before calling this function.</span></span></span>

    >>> import traceback​>>> try:>>>      raise Exception('This is the error message.')>>> except:>>>      with open('errorInfo.txt', 'w') as error_file:>>>          error_file.write(traceback.format_exc())>>>      print('The traceback info was written to errorInfo.txt.')116The traceback info was written to errorInfo.txt.

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="38ca5b3742964c329ce9ef83afd97137"><span data-offset-key="38ca5b3742964c329ce9ef83afd97137:0">The 116 is the return value from the write() method, since 116 characters were written to the file. The traceback text was written to errorInfo.txt.</span></span></span>

    Traceback (most recent call last):  File "<pyshell#28>", line 2, in <module>Exception: This is the error message.

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c19f385846254a399ca3d90e7ec755db"><span data-offset-key="c19f385846254a399ca3d90e7ec755db:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0671a685bc9845edb3a00d341de52811"><span data-offset-key="0671a685bc9845edb3a00d341de52811:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="a6e36c831c8543f3b88c41dd3d6af480"><span data-offset-key="a6e36c831c8543f3b88c41dd3d6af480:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9499a09f4b7a467697beb979c6bad0b2"><span data-offset-key="9499a09f4b7a467697beb979c6bad0b2:0">Assertions</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a78fc1fa45514417ab86be402503db9e"><span data-offset-key="a78fc1fa45514417ab86be402503db9e:0">An assertion is a sanity check to make sure your code isn’t doing something obviously wrong. These sanity checks are performed by assert statements. If the sanity check fails, then an AssertionError exception is raised. In code, an assert statement consists of the following:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1c2a72a4deed419e959b97907aef6728"><span data-offset-key="1c2a72a4deed419e959b97907aef6728:0">The assert keyword</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d2232d9c52114b588d9c547c59c9d4f3"><span data-offset-key="d2232d9c52114b588d9c547c59c9d4f3:0">A condition (that is, an expression that evaluates to True or False)</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b8d8aa91e9c4a52bb47b9a3644d080a"><span data-offset-key="1b8d8aa91e9c4a52bb47b9a3644d080a:0">A comma</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1f0e658fc5c541108a5f684b7ad93609"><span data-offset-key="1f0e658fc5c541108a5f684b7ad93609:0">A string to display when the condition is False</span></span></span>

    >>> pod_bay_door_status = 'open'​>>> assert pod_bay_door_status == 'open', 'The pod bay doors need to be "open".'​>>> pod_bay_door_status = 'I\'m sorry, Dave. I\'m afraid I can\'t do that.'​>>> assert pod_bay_door_status == 'open', 'The pod bay doors need to be "open".'​Traceback (most recent call last):  File "<pyshell#10>", line 1, in <module>    assert pod_bay_door_status == 'open', 'The pod bay doors need to be "open".'AssertionError: The pod bay doors need to be "open".

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cadca206ce6549ada13b87866962fa18"><span data-offset-key="cadca206ce6549ada13b87866962fa18:0">In plain English, an assert statement says, “I assert that this condition holds true, and if not, there is a bug somewhere in the program.” Unlike exceptions, your code should not handle assert statements with try and except; if an assert fails, your program should crash. By failing fast like this, you shorten the time between the original cause of the bug and when you first notice the bug. This will reduce the amount of code you will have to check before finding the code that’s causing the bug.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ea3733c927ac4a958fd462902e715bef"><span data-offset-key="ea3733c927ac4a958fd462902e715bef:0">Disabling Assertions</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9fddac431023494da321663c1ec11169"><span data-offset-key="9fddac431023494da321663c1ec11169:0">Assertions can be disabled by passing the -O option when running Python.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fc4dd30f16534ea882444b4a9a20935f"><span data-offset-key="fc4dd30f16534ea882444b4a9a20935f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="74bfc98c4c6448dca63acaf6c5e25c71"><span data-offset-key="74bfc98c4c6448dca63acaf6c5e25c71:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="0e644b7e4477498a810ffeb8a06e56e1"><span data-offset-key="0e644b7e4477498a810ffeb8a06e56e1:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ef73a356c7dd4957b442dfa31ebdd634"><span data-offset-key="ef73a356c7dd4957b442dfa31ebdd634:0">Logging</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9688feec1f394c6090c619baae2a795b"><span data-offset-key="9688feec1f394c6090c619baae2a795b:0">To enable the logging module to display log messages on your screen as your program runs, copy the following to the top of your program (but under the \#! python shebang line):</span></span></span>

    import logging​logging.basicConfig(level=logging.DEBUG, format=' %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s- %(message)s')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="735487fc7ed349d1acd2dfb5988817dc"><span data-offset-key="735487fc7ed349d1acd2dfb5988817dc:0">Say you wrote a function to calculate the factorial of a number. In mathematics, factorial 4 is 1 × 2 × 3 × 4, or 24. Factorial 7 is 1 × 2 × 3 × 4 × 5 × 6 × 7, or 5,040. Open a new file editor window and enter the following code. It has a bug in it, but you will also enter several log messages to help yourself figure out what is going wrong. Save the program as factorialLog.py.</span></span></span>

    >>> import logging>>>>>> logging.basicConfig(level=logging.DEBUG, format=' %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s- %(message)s')>>>>>> logging.debug('Start of program')>>>>>> def factorial(n):>>>>>>     logging.debug('Start of factorial(%s)' % (n))>>>     total = 1>>>>>>     for i in range(1, n + 1):>>>         total *= i>>>         logging.debug('i is ' + str(i) + ', total is ' + str(total))>>>>>>     logging.debug('End of factorial(%s)' % (n))>>>>>>     return total>>>>>> print(factorial(5))>>> logging.debug('End of program')2015-05-23 16:20:12,664 - DEBUG - Start of program2015-05-23 16:20:12,664 - DEBUG - Start of factorial(5)2015-05-23 16:20:12,665 - DEBUG - i is 0, total is 02015-05-23 16:20:12,668 - DEBUG - i is 1, total is 02015-05-23 16:20:12,670 - DEBUG - i is 2, total is 02015-05-23 16:20:12,673 - DEBUG - i is 3, total is 02015-05-23 16:20:12,675 - DEBUG - i is 4, total is 02015-05-23 16:20:12,678 - DEBUG - i is 5, total is 02015-05-23 16:20:12,680 - DEBUG - End of factorial(5)02015-05-23 16:20:12,684 - DEBUG - End of program

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d7eb7c9fa10c458296bff8234b5825f4"><span data-offset-key="d7eb7c9fa10c458296bff8234b5825f4:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ec91412bad904988acd7fc2d4b539b94"><span data-offset-key="ec91412bad904988acd7fc2d4b539b94:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="c0ad6f7ba10748b4a94f8195381fe9f3"><span data-offset-key="c0ad6f7ba10748b4a94f8195381fe9f3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7023682cdc374bfe8bb7f8e2f79ae9b8"><span data-offset-key="7023682cdc374bfe8bb7f8e2f79ae9b8:0">Logging Levels</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a920bc4e491e411a877b19328c2c3b58"><span data-offset-key="a920bc4e491e411a877b19328c2c3b58:0">Logging levels provide a way to categorize your log messages by importance. There are five logging levels, described in Table 10-1 from least to most important. Messages can be logged at each level using a different logging function.</span></span></span>

<table><colgroup><col style="width: 33%" /><col style="width: 33%" /><col style="width: 33%" /></colgroup><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2a9fbf7481224408864b0cb5938e5b3b"><span data-offset-key="2a9fbf7481224408864b0cb5938e5b3b:0">Level</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="31aeb2f15d1c46618e2a622572063cc3"><span data-offset-key="31aeb2f15d1c46618e2a622572063cc3:0">Logging Function</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4754570a919c4f22bafde3adb5f53d63"><span data-offset-key="4754570a919c4f22bafde3adb5f53d63:0">Description</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d023a972db834e3c80b4c6c4f25ce1c7"><span data-offset-key="d023a972db834e3c80b4c6c4f25ce1c7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">DEBUG</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1a1e5601c43e4cae9ab220b792130e45"><span data-offset-key="1a1e5601c43e4cae9ab220b792130e45:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">logging.debug()</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="551eab55d5444379ac4d6d750fcbecfd"><span data-offset-key="551eab55d5444379ac4d6d750fcbecfd:0">The lowest level. Used for small details. Usually you care about these messages only when diagnosing problems.</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dcc163717e8c4c36983a060ba3001209"><span data-offset-key="dcc163717e8c4c36983a060ba3001209:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">INFO</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ca50b2be18e948b0b446d3cba6beaa10"><span data-offset-key="ca50b2be18e948b0b446d3cba6beaa10:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">logging.info()</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="00b906cbd69b4b8894bf2bb0e1ecd6ae"><span data-offset-key="00b906cbd69b4b8894bf2bb0e1ecd6ae:0">Used to record information on general events in your program or confirm that things are working at their point in the program.</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c8c0f701ffa94d0485a426e2ab70e0ec"><span data-offset-key="c8c0f701ffa94d0485a426e2ab70e0ec:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">WARNING</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="441542e373aa49c1aca9991fa44e17c2"><span data-offset-key="441542e373aa49c1aca9991fa44e17c2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">logging.warning()</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2c6cb22096cc446d86bdb9151c118ab2"><span data-offset-key="2c6cb22096cc446d86bdb9151c118ab2:0">Used to indicate a potential problem that doesn’t prevent the program from working but might do so in the future.</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0280eee73ef0451fa847f5ca730304f3"><span data-offset-key="0280eee73ef0451fa847f5ca730304f3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ERROR</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="408e7cc2a7204181bf19f7697b7f2029"><span data-offset-key="408e7cc2a7204181bf19f7697b7f2029:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">logging.error()</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d29ad2f887824793bd13249ddd12b559"><span data-offset-key="d29ad2f887824793bd13249ddd12b559:0">Used to record an error that caused the program to fail to do something.</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c154a3439bed4a23b76957a92ac52379"><span data-offset-key="c154a3439bed4a23b76957a92ac52379:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">CRITICAL</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1c4e803f1dfe4074a53e3e59884bf7fd"><span data-offset-key="1c4e803f1dfe4074a53e3e59884bf7fd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">logging.critical()</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="708410f9ab934034883e55aaf3c49c44"><span data-offset-key="708410f9ab934034883e55aaf3c49c44:0">The highest level. Used to indicate a fatal error that has caused or is about to cause the program to stop running entirely.</span></span></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bbd738bed05540db95dfb8ded03678e1"><span data-offset-key="bbd738bed05540db95dfb8ded03678e1:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9196e6908c54460ea6f7f4c32a93221a"><span data-offset-key="9196e6908c54460ea6f7f4c32a93221a:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="f467eef0a1cc43af92e4668803cb29ae"><span data-offset-key="f467eef0a1cc43af92e4668803cb29ae:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fa2943e79cb54027b5141868f215ec94"><span data-offset-key="fa2943e79cb54027b5141868f215ec94:0">Disabling Logging</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d7ae9cffd2224ba4991ea26167a2090f"><span data-offset-key="d7ae9cffd2224ba4991ea26167a2090f:0">After you’ve debugged your program, you probably don’t want all these log messages cluttering the screen. The logging.disable() function disables these so that you don’t have to go into your program and remove all the logging calls by hand.</span></span></span>

    >>> import logging​>>> logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format=' %(asctime)s -%(levelname)s - %(message)s')​>>> logging.critical('Critical error! Critical error!')2015-05-22 11:10:48,054 - CRITICAL - Critical error! Critical error!​>>> logging.disable(logging.CRITICAL)​>>> logging.critical('Critical error! Critical error!')​>>> logging.error('Error! Error!')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="35f6d193b2ef444fbec9e4841ec18caf"><span data-offset-key="35f6d193b2ef444fbec9e4841ec18caf:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/Web-Dev-Collaborative/python-cheatsheet#python-cheatsheet" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2f4843f994c044499f76d62707cfc241"><span data-offset-key="2f4843f994c044499f76d62707cfc241:0"><em>Return to the Top</em></span></span></a><span data-key="5b56736a3b6b414c80efad6406b85f87"><span data-offset-key="5b56736a3b6b414c80efad6406b85f87:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

###
